## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart TD
    S1([Package Event])
    S1 --> P1[process_back_order_exception]
    P1 --> D1{has_expected_state == DELIVERED?}
    D1 -- No --> D2{event_code == BACKORDER_RECEIVED?}
    D2 -- Yes --> A1[post_put_container_exception EXCEPTION_BACKORDER]
    D2 -- No --> D3{event_code == BACKORDER_CLEARED?}
    D3 -- Yes --> C1[clear_exceptions]
    D3 -- No --> END1([End])
    C1 --> E1{get_event_on_trip_leg_location?}
    E1 -- Yes --> C1a[clear_exceptions short/misrouted/missing/held]
    E1 -- No --> C1b[continue]
    C1 --> E2{event_code in ARRIVED or DEPARTED?}
    E2 -- Yes --> C1c[clear_exceptions misrouted/lost/held/short/recycled/missing]
    E2 -- No --> E3{event_code == DELIVERED?}
    E3 -- Yes --> C1d[clear_exceptions held/recycled/lost/missing/misrouted/short/transship/missed_pickup/off_schedule/behind_schedule]
    E3 -- No --> E4{event_code == BACKORDER_CLEARED?}
    E4 -- Yes --> C1e[clear_exceptions backorder]
    C1 --> O1[ocean_missed_pickup_exception_cancel_or_clear]

    S1 --> O2[ocean_off_schedule_exception_by_event]
    O2 --> V1{valid_exception_for_off_schedule?}
    V1 -- No --> END2([End])
    V1 -- Yes --> G1[__get_trip_leg_by_location]
    G1 -- NoTrip --> END2
    G1 -- TripFound --> V2{__is_event_off_schedule?}
    V2 -- Yes --> A2[post_ocean_container_exception EXCEPTION_OFF_SCHEDULE]
    V2 -- No --> END2

    S1 --> M1[ocean_missed_pickup_exception_by_trip_leg]
    M1 --> V3{valid_exception_for_missed_pickup?}
    V3 -- No --> END3([End])
    V3 -- Yes --> L1[_load_containers_for_trip_leg]
    L1 --> FOR1{for each container}
    FOR1 --> M2[ocean_missed_pickup_exception]
    M2 --> V4{origin_arrived_ts or origin_departed_ts is None?}
    V4 -- Yes --> G2[__get_trip_leg_by_id origin_planned_trip_leg_id]
    G2 -- TripNull --> END3
    G2 -- TripFound --> V5{scheduled_origin_pickup_window.upper exists?}
    V5 -- Yes --> A3[post_ocean_container_exception EXCEPTION_MISSED_PICKUP event_ts=window.upper]
    V5 -- No --> END3

    S1 --> T1[ocean_unplanned_transship_exception_by_trip_leg]
    T1 --> V6{valid_exception_for_transship?}
    V6 -- No --> END4([End])
    V6 -- Yes --> L2[_load_containers_for_trip_leg]
    L2 --> FOR2{for each container}
    FOR2 --> T2[ocean_unplanned_transship_exception]
    T2 --> G3[__trip_leg_data_store.get_trip_legs_for_container]
    G3 --> Cnt1[_count_port_to_port_trips]
    Cnt1 --> V7{port_to_port_count >= TRANSSHIP_MIN_PORT_TO_PORT_TRIPS?}
    V7 -- Yes --> A4[post_ocean_container_exception EXCEPTION_TRANSSHIP]
    V7 -- No --> END4
```
